  <!-- SECTION 3: THE GAP NOBODY TALKS ABOUT -->

  <section class="gap-section section-dark-mid">

    <div class="container">

      <h2>AI only gets you started.<br>It doesn't get you finished.</h2>

      <p class="lede">Every AI platform shows you the beginning, the fast prototype, the working demo, and the exciting parts. But nobody shows you what happens after.</p>

      <div class="gap-stat">

        For every hour AI builds, it takes <strong>four to five human hours</strong> to make that code production-ready.

      </div>

      <p class="closing">Drytis is built for that gap.</p>

    </div>

  </section>

  <!-- SECTION 4: WHAT DRYTIS ACTUALLY IS -->

  <section class="what-section">

    <div class="container">

      <h2>Once AI completes its part, Drytis gives you the human engineer who reviews it, tests it, and finishes it right.</h2>

      <p>That's the only thing that matters here.</p>

    </div>

  </section>

  <!-- SECTION 5: HOW IT WORKS -->

  <section class="how-section section-soft">

    <div class="container">

      <h2>Here's what actually happens.</h2>

      <div class="how-steps">

        <div class="how-step">

          <div><h3>You build with AI.</h3><p>Describe what you want. AI builds fast. Gets you most of the way there.</p></div>

        </div>

        <div class="how-step">

          <div><h3>AI completes its part.</h3><p>But bugs, security gaps, and architecture problems still need a human to catch.</p></div>

        </div>

        <div class="how-step">

          <div><h3>A real human engineer steps in.</h3><p>They read your build. They see every decision you made. They pick up without you explaining a thing.</p></div>

        </div>

        <div class="how-step">

          <div><h3>You stay in the loop.</h3><p>Watch them work in real time. Send messages. Jump on a call. You're never out of the picture.</p></div>

        </div>

        <div class="how-step final">

          <div><h3>You build something that actually works.</h3><p>Tested. Secure. Production-ready. Not a prototype. A product.</p></div>

        </div>

      </div>

      <a href="#" class="btn btn-outline">See How It Works →</a>

    </div>

  </section>

<script>

(function(){

  const RING_LINES = [

    { label: "You had an idea." },

    { label: "AI gave you confidence." },

    { label: "You built something." },

    { label: "Then it got complicated." },

    { label: "You got stuck." },

    { label: "And you realised something." }

  ];

  const NUM_RINGS = RING_LINES.length;

  const CENTER = 320;

  const R_MIN = 70;

  const R_MAX = 300;

  const svgNS = 'http://www.w3.org/2000/svg';

  const STOPS = [

    { p: 0.0, c: [214, 216, 199] },

    { p: 0.4, c: [169, 178, 154] },

    { p: 0.7, c: [143, 161, 132] },

    { p: 1.0, c: [165, 68, 80] }

  ];

  function lerpColor(p) {

    for (let i = 0; i < STOPS.length - 1; i++) {

      const a = STOPS[i], b = STOPS[i + 1];

      if (p >= a.p && p <= b.p) {

        const t = (p - a.p) / (b.p - a.p || 1);

        const c = a.c.map((v, idx) => Math.round(v + (b.c[idx] - v) * t));

        return `rgb(${c[0]},${c[1]},${c[2]})`;

      }

    }

    const last = STOPS[STOPS.length - 1].c;

    return `rgb(${last[0]},${last[1]},${last[2]})`;

  }

  const ANCHOR_ANGLES_DEG = [-90, -28, 145, -152, 42, -160];

  const svg = document.getElementById('orbit-svg');

  const stage = document.getElementById('orbit-stage');

  const rings = [];

  const spinWraps = [];

  const pills = [];

  for (let i = 0; i < NUM_RINGS; i++) {

    const radius = R_MIN + (R_MAX - R_MIN) * (i / (NUM_RINGS - 1));

    const ring = document.createElementNS(svgNS, 'circle');

    ring.setAttribute('cx', CENTER);

    ring.setAttribute('cy', CENTER);

    ring.setAttribute('r', radius);

    ring.setAttribute('class', 'orbit-ring');

    svg.appendChild(ring);

    rings.push(ring);

    const wrap = document.createElement('div');

    wrap.className = 'orbit-spin-wrap';

    const size = (radius / R_MAX) * 100;

    wrap.style.width = size + '%';

    wrap.style.height = size + '%';

    wrap.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%)';

    wrap.style.animation = `orbitspin ${16 + i * 5}s linear infinite`;

    const dot = document.createElement('div');

    dot.className = 'orbit-spin-dot';

    wrap.appendChild(dot);

    stage.appendChild(wrap);

    spinWraps.push({ wrap, dot });

    const angle = ANCHOR_ANGLES_DEG[i] * Math.PI / 180;

    const pctRadius = (radius / R_MAX) * 50;

    const px = 50 + pctRadius * Math.cos(angle);

    const py = 50 + pctRadius * Math.sin(angle);

    const pill = document.createElement('div');

    pill.className = 'orbit-pill';

    pill.style.left = px + '%';

    pill.style.top = py + '%';

    pill.innerHTML = `<span class="orbit-pill-dot"></span><span class="orbit-pill-label">${RING_LINES[i].label}</span>`;

    stage.appendChild(pill);

    pills.push(pill);

  }

  const styleTag = document.createElement('style');

  styleTag.textContent = `@keyframes orbitspin { from { transform: translate(-50%,-50%) rotate(0deg); } to { transform: translate(-50%,-50%) rotate(360deg); } }`;

  document.head.appendChild(styleTag);

  const eyebrowEl = document.getElementById('journey-eyebrow');

  const section = document.getElementById('drytis-journey');

  function clamp(v, min, max) { return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, v)); }

  function smoothstep(t) { t = clamp(t, 0, 1); return t * t * (3 - 2 * t); }

  // NUM_SEGMENTS here just paces the eyebrow + 6 rings across the play duration

  // (no "final" segment anymore -- that message moved to its own section below).

  const PLAY_SEGMENTS = NUM_RINGS + 1;

  function update(progress) {

    const seg = 1 / PLAY_SEGMENTS;

    const eyebrowP = smoothstep(progress / (seg * 0.7));

    eyebrowEl.style.opacity = clamp(eyebrowP, 0, 1) * (progress < seg * 1.5 ? 1 : Math.max(0.35, 1 - (progress - seg * 1.5) / seg));

    for (let i = 0; i < NUM_RINGS; i++) {

      const segStart = (i + 1) * seg;

      const localP = smoothstep((progress - segStart) / (seg * 0.85));

      const color = lerpColor(progress);

      rings[i].style.opacity = localP * 0.9;

      rings[i].style.stroke = color;

      rings[i].style.filter = localP > 0.05 ? `drop-shadow(0 0 ${4 + localP * 5}px ${color})` : 'none';

      const scale = 0.92 + localP * 0.08;

      rings[i].style.transform = `scale(${scale})`;

      spinWraps[i].wrap.style.opacity = localP * 0.9;

      spinWraps[i].dot.style.background = color;

      spinWraps[i].dot.style.boxShadow = `0 0 6px ${color}`;

      pills[i].style.opacity = localP;

      pills[i].style.transform = `translate(-50%, -50%) scale(${0.85 + localP * 0.15})`;

      pills[i].style.background = color;

      pills[i].querySelector('.orbit-pill-dot').style.background = 'rgba(20,38,28,0.35)';

      pills[i].querySelector('.orbit-pill-label').style.color = progress > 0.7 ? '#FAF3F0' : '#14261C';

    }

  }

  // Plays once, automatically, the moment the section is actually in view --

  // no scrolling required to drive it. This replaced an 800vh scroll-jacked

  // version that people found required too much scrolling to get through.

  const PLAY_DURATION_MS = 11000;

  let hasPlayed = false;

  function play() {

    if (hasPlayed) return;

    hasPlayed = true;

    const start = performance.now();

    function frame(now) {

      const progress = clamp((now - start) / PLAY_DURATION_MS, 0, 1);

      update(progress);

      if (progress < 1) requestAnimationFrame(frame);

    }

    requestAnimationFrame(frame);

  }

  update(0); // render the resting/start state immediately, before it plays

  if ('IntersectionObserver' in window) {

    const io = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {

      entries.forEach((entry) => { if (entry.isIntersecting) play(); });

    }, { threshold: 0.35 });

    io.observe(section);

  } else {

    play(); // very old browsers: just play it

  }

})();

// ---------- Code Patch: hover-triggered typing + syntax highlight ----------

(function(){

  const CODE = `// routes/auth.js

import express from 'express';

import { hashPassword } from '../utils/crypto.js';

import { db } from '../db/client.js';

const router = express.Router();

router.post('/signup', async (req, res) => {

  const { email, password } = req.body;

  if (!email || !password) {

    return res.status(400).json({

      error: 'Email and password required'

    });

  }

  const existing = await db.users.findOne({ email });

  if (existing) {

    return res.status(409).json({

      error: 'Account already exists'

    });

  }

  const hashed = await hashPassword(password);

  const user = await db.users.create({ email, hashed });

  return res.status(201).json({ id: user.id });

});

export default router;`;

  const KEYWORDS = ['import','from','export','default','const','let','async','await','return','if','else','new','try','catch','function'];

  function escapeHtml(s) {

    return s.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');

  }

  function highlight(text) {

    let out = escapeHtml(text);

    // comments

    out = out.replace(/(\/\/[^\n]*)/g, '<span class="hl-cm">$1</span>');

    // strings (single-quoted, simple demo-grade matching)

    out = out.replace(/('[^'\n]*')/g, '<span class="hl-str">$1</span>');

    // keywords

    const kwPattern = new RegExp('\\b(' + KEYWORDS.join('|') + ')\\b', 'g');

    out = out.replace(kwPattern, '<span class="hl-kw">$1</span>');

    return out;

  }

  const wrap = document.getElementById('code-patch-wrap');

  const body = document.getElementById('code-patch-body');

  const hint = document.getElementById('code-patch-hint');

  const preview = document.getElementById('code-preview');

  if (!wrap || !body) return;

  const CYCLE_MS = 15000; // full loop length: type -> hold -> reset -> repeat

  const MIN_HOLD_MS = 1500; // always hold the finished code for at least this long

  const RESET_PAUSE_MS = 500; // brief blank pause before the next type-out begins

  let started = false;

  let timer = null;

  function cycle() {

    const cycleStart = Date.now();

    let i = 0;

    hint.textContent = 'Generating…';

    body.innerHTML = '';

    if (preview) preview.classList.remove('visible');

    clearInterval(timer);

    timer = setInterval(() => {

      i += 2; // characters per tick, for a natural typing speed

      const slice = CODE.slice(0, i);

      body.innerHTML = highlight(slice) + '<span class="code-cursor">&nbsp;</span>';

      if (i >= CODE.length) {

        clearInterval(timer);

        body.innerHTML = highlight(CODE);

        hint.textContent = 'Generated by an engineer-reviewed AI build';

        if (preview) preview.classList.add('visible');

        const elapsed = Date.now() - cycleStart;

        const holdTime = Math.max(CYCLE_MS - elapsed, MIN_HOLD_MS);

        setTimeout(() => {

          // back to the original, empty window

          body.innerHTML = '';

          hint.textContent = 'Hover or tap to watch it write';

          if (preview) preview.classList.remove('visible');

          setTimeout(cycle, RESET_PAUSE_MS);

        }, holdTime);

      }

    }, 14);

  }

  function beginIfNeeded() {

    if (!started) {

      started = true;

      cycle();

    }

  }

  wrap.addEventListener('mouseenter', beginIfNeeded);

  // touchscreens don't fire mouseenter from a tap -- trigger the same way on touch

  wrap.addEventListener('touchstart', beginIfNeeded, { passive: true });

})();

// ---------- Hero prompt bar: suggestion chips fill the input ----------

(function(){

  const input = document.getElementById('hero-prompt-input');

  const chips = document.querySelectorAll('.hero-chip');

  if (!input || !chips.length) return;

  chips.forEach((chip) => {

    chip.addEventListener('click', () => {

      input.value = chip.textContent;

      input.focus();

    });

  });

  // NOTE: there's no real Studio backend behind this yet -- "send" is a visual

  // placeholder until that's built. Wire this up to the real build flow later.

})();

</script>

<script>

(function(){

  var toggle = document.getElementById('nav-toggle');

  var panel = document.getElementById('nav-mobile-panel');

  if (!toggle || !panel) return;

  toggle.addEventListener('click', function(){

    var isOpen = toggle.classList.toggle('open');

    panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);

    toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');

  });

  panel.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(a){

    a.addEventListener('click', function(){

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    });

  });

  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){

    if (window.innerWidth > 860) {

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

})();

</script>

</body>

<script>

(function(){

  // ------------------------------------------------------------------

  // NOTE: this is a client-side, keyword-based heuristic for demo purposes.

  // It gives an illustrative tier suggestion + placeholder time/cost ranges.

  // For real production use, replace `recommendTier()` with a call to your

  // own backend (which can safely call an LLM with your API key server-side

  // and apply real scoping logic) rather than hardcoding estimates client-side.

  // ------------------------------------------------------------------

  const TIER_INFO = {

    studio: {

      name: 'Drytis 5.1',

      time: '1–2 weeks to a working prototype',

      cost: '$25/month',

      reason: "this sounds like an early-stage idea: pure AI building is the fastest way to get a working prototype in front of yourself or early users.",

      link: 'pricing.html#studio'

    },

    edge: {

      name: 'Edge',

      time: '2–4 weeks to production-ready',

      cost: 'From $2.80/M tokens + engineer time (agreed upfront)',

      reason: "it sounds like you've already got something built and have hit real limits: bugs, architecture, or things AI can't safely finish. That's exactly where an engineer picks up.",

      link: 'pricing.html#edge'

    },

    albert: {

      name: 'Albert',

      time: 'Ongoing engagement, scoped to your roadmap',

      cost: 'From $13.75/M tokens',

      reason: "this sounds like a serious, higher-stakes build where the cost of a wrong technical decision is high. That's where senior engineering guidance matters most.",

      link: 'pricing.html#albert'

    }

  };

  const KEYWORDS = {

    albert: ['scale', 'scaling', 'enterprise', 'compliance', 'funded', 'funding', 'infrastructure', 'millions of users', 'bank', 'healthcare', 'security-critical', 'investors'],

    edge: ['built', 'prototype is done', 'stuck', 'bug', 'bugs', 'launch', 'production', 'users', 'broken', 'mvp', 'live', 'crashing', 'fix'],

    studio: ['idea', 'just starting', 'new idea', 'simple', 'no code', 'beginner', 'first time', 'concept', 'thinking about', 'want to build']

  };

  function recommendTier(text) {

    const lower = text.toLowerCase();

    const scores = { studio: 0, edge: 0, albert: 0 };

    Object.keys(KEYWORDS).forEach((tier) => {

      KEYWORDS[tier].forEach((kw) => {

        if (lower.includes(kw)) scores[tier] += 1;

      });

    });

    if (scores.albert > 0 && scores.albert >= scores.edge && scores.albert >= scores.studio) return 'albert';

    if (scores.edge > 0 && scores.edge >= scores.studio) return 'edge';

    if (scores.studio > 0) return 'studio';

    // default: no strong signal, assume early-stage idea

    return 'studio';

  }

  const messagesEl = document.getElementById('chat-messages');

  const inputEl = document.getElementById('chat-input');

  const sendEl = document.getElementById('chat-send');

  function scrollToBottom() {

    messagesEl.scrollTop = messagesEl.scrollHeight;

  }

  function addUserMessage(text) {

    const row = document.createElement('div');

    row.className = 'msg-row user';

    row.innerHTML = `<div class="msg-bubble"></div>`;

    row.querySelector('.msg-bubble').textContent = text;

    messagesEl.appendChild(row);

    scrollToBottom();

  }

  function addTypingIndicator() {

    const row = document.createElement('div');

    row.className = 'msg-row assistant';

    row.id = 'typing-row';

    row.innerHTML = `

      <div class="msg-avatar"><div class="dot"></div></div>

      <div class="msg-bubble"><div class="typing-dots"><span></span><span></span><span></span></div></div>

    `;

    messagesEl.appendChild(row);

    scrollToBottom();

  }

  function removeTypingIndicator() {

    const row = document.getElementById('typing-row');

    if (row) row.remove();

  }

  function addAssistantRecommendation(tierKey) {

    const tier = TIER_INFO[tierKey];

    const row = document.createElement('div');

    row.className = 'msg-row assistant';

    row.innerHTML = `

      <div class="msg-avatar"><div class="dot"></div></div>

      <div class="msg-bubble">

        <span class="tier-tag">${tier.name}</span>

        <div>Based on what you described, ${tier.reason}</div>

        <div class="estimate-line">Estimated timeline: <strong>${tier.time}</strong></div>

        <div class="estimate-line">Estimated cost: <strong>${tier.cost}</strong></div>

        <a class="estimate-cta" href="${tier.link}">See ${tier.name} pricing →</a>

      </div>

    `;

    messagesEl.appendChild(row);

    scrollToBottom();

  }

  function handleSend() {

    const text = inputEl.value.trim();

    if (!text) return;

    addUserMessage(text);

    inputEl.value = '';

    sendEl.disabled = true;

    addTypingIndicator();

    setTimeout(() => {

      removeTypingIndicator();

      const tierKey = recommendTier(text);

      addAssistantRecommendation(tierKey);

      sendEl.disabled = false;

    }, 900);

  }

  sendEl.addEventListener('click', handleSend);

  inputEl.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {

    if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSend();

  });

})();

</script>

<script>

(function(){

  var toggle = document.getElementById('nav-toggle');

  var panel = document.getElementById('nav-mobile-panel');

  if (!toggle || !panel) return;

  toggle.addEventListener('click', function(){

    var isOpen = toggle.classList.toggle('open');

    panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);

    toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');

  });

  panel.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(a){

    a.addEventListener('click', function(){

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    });

  });

  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){

    if (window.innerWidth > 860) {

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

})();

</script>

  <section class="feat-hero">

    <div class="container">

      <h1>Built for the moment<span class="accent">a human takes over.</span></h1>

      <p>Everything is ready the moment you log in. No setup or configuration required.</p>

    </div>

  </section>

  <!-- 01 THE ENVIRONMENT -->

  <section class="feat-section">

    <div class="container">

      <h2>Your workspace stays exactly as you left it.</h2>

      <div class="env-grid">

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">&gt;_</span><h3>Terminal</h3><p>A real shell with real commands.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">[F]</span><h3>Files</h3><p>Your codebase intact.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">◎</span><h3>Preview</h3><p>Live changes that are shareable before deployment.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">&lt;/&gt;</span><h3>IDE</h3><p>A full editor.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">Y</span><h3>Repositories</h3><p>Every commit and branch gets tracked.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">▪</span><h3>Database</h3><p>Built in and already connected.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">[•]</span><h3>Env Files</h3><p>To carry the secrets through the handoff.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">⚙</span><h3>Services</h3><p>Backend services, running alongside your build.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">↗</span><h3>Proxy</h3><p>Domains, endpoints, and routing, all in one place.</p></div>

        <div class="env-card"><span class="env-icon">◷</span><h3>Snapshots</h3><p>One click back to what worked.</p></div>

      </div>

    </div>

  </section>

  <!-- 02 THE HUMAN LAYER -->

  <section class="feat-section on-dark">

    <div class="container">

      <h2>When AI isn't enough, an engineer is.</h2>

      <p class="lede">You'll know what's happening and why, the whole time. Nothing runs somewhere you can't see it.</p>

<script>

(function(){

  var toggle = document.getElementById('nav-toggle');

  var panel = document.getElementById('nav-mobile-panel');

  if (!toggle || !panel) return;

  toggle.addEventListener('click', function(){

    var isOpen = toggle.classList.toggle('open');

    panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);

    toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');

  });

  panel.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(a){

    a.addEventListener('click', function(){

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    });

  });

  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){

    if (window.innerWidth > 860) {

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

})();

</script>

<script>

(function(){

  var toggle = document.getElementById('nav-toggle');

  var panel = document.getElementById('nav-mobile-panel');

  if (!toggle || !panel) return;

  toggle.addEventListener('click', function(){

    var isOpen = toggle.classList.toggle('open');

    panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);

    toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');

  });

  panel.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(a){

    a.addEventListener('click', function(){

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    });

  });

  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){

    if (window.innerWidth > 860) {

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

})();

</script>

  <section class="page-hero">

    <div class="container">

      <h1>FAQs.</h1>

    </div>

  </section>

  <!-- ACCORDION -->

  <section class="faq-section">

    <div class="container">

      <div class="faq-list">

        <details class="faq-item" open>

          <summary>Do I need to be technical to use Drytis?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">No. That's exactly who this is built for. You describe what you want. The AI and engineers handle everything else.</div>

        </details>

        <details class="faq-item">

          <summary>What happens when AI gets stuck?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">On Edge and Albert, a qualified engineer is automatically connected. They read your project and get to work. You don't have to explain anything.</div>

        </details>

        <details class="faq-item">

          <summary>Who are the engineers?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">Experienced, qualified engineers. On Edge, senior engineers. On Albert, the most experienced in their field. All vetted. All accountable.</div>

        </details>

        <details class="faq-item">

          <summary>How do I know what it'll cost?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">On Edge and Albert, the engineering cost is agreed with you before any human work starts. You know before they start. Always.</div>

        </details>

        <details class="faq-item">

          <summary>What if I don't like what the engineer builds?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">You watch in real time. Message them. Redirect them. You know what's happening before it's done.</div>

        </details>

        <details class="faq-item">

          <summary>How is this different from hiring a freelancer?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">The engineer already knows your project: no briefing, no re-explaining. And you know the cost upfront. No open-ended invoices.</div>

        </details>

        <details class="faq-item">

          <summary>Can I start on Studio and move to Edge?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">Yes. Start wherever you are. Move up when you're ready.</div>

        </details>

        <details class="faq-item">

          <summary>What does Edge actually cost?<span class="icon">+</span></summary>

          <div class="faq-answer">It depends on what needs to be done. But the number is agreed before anyone starts work. No surprises.</div>

        </details>

      </div>

    </div>

  </section>

<script>

(function(){

  var toggle = document.getElementById('nav-toggle');

  var panel = document.getElementById('nav-mobile-panel');

  if (!toggle || !panel) return;

  toggle.addEventListener('click', function(){

    var isOpen = toggle.classList.toggle('open');

    panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);

    toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');

  });

  panel.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(a){

    a.addEventListener('click', function(){

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    });

  });

  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){

    if (window.innerWidth > 860) {

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

})();

</script>

</body>

<script>

(function(){

  var toggle = document.getElementById('nav-toggle');

  var panel = document.getElementById('nav-mobile-panel');

  if (!toggle || !panel) return;

  toggle.addEventListener('click', function(){

    var isOpen = toggle.classList.toggle('open');

    panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);

    toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');

  });

  panel.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function(a){

    a.addEventListener('click', function(){

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    });

  });

  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){

    if (window.innerWidth > 860) {

      toggle.classList.remove('open');

      panel.classList.remove('open');

      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

})();

</script>

</body>

</html>
